msg:Every year when I go to Putuo Mountain, I basically choose to stay at Putuo Villa for one night because it is relatively close to Puji Temple. This stay was extremely disappointing. First, we ate at the restaurant. My daughter ordered a broad bean stew. When she was about to finish eating, she discovered that all the broad beans in the chili were moldy. Suddenly I felt goose bumps, nausea, and vomiting. We checked in with a residence permit for Hong Kong and Macao residents, but the waiter questioned me and asked me if I had a return permit? I'm confused. Nowadays, residence permit is used here to handle banking business, buy a house, and provide medical and social security. A residence permit is required for taking trains, planes and other activities. The residence permit for Hong Kong and Macao residents is the same as the second-generation ID card. Then the waiter gave me a tail room and opened it. The room was super hot. It was obvious that no one had stayed in the room for a long time. After raising questions immediately, I was given another room. The room facilities are very old and the TV cannot be turned on. There is a foul smell in the toilet sewer.
